                remaining adhyāyas based on K. Cleaned up the files, removing
                transcription codes.</change>
            <change when="2024-11-27" who="Dominik Wujastyk">Split the uttaratantra files
                from 31-end into 31-44 and 45-66. Updated all the file and folder names
                accordingly.</change>
            <change when="2025-05-30" who="Deepro Chakraborty and Dominik Wujastyk">We
                copied chapter xml:id 6.24 "pratiśyāya" from
                provisional-edition_uttaratantra-01-30.txt to this file,
                provisional-edition_uttaratantra-45-66.txt, between svaropaghāta and krimi
                (xml:id 53 and 54). This is the position of the pratiśyāya chapter in the
                Nepalese MSS.</change>

                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 45: draft edition based on MS K]</head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.1">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.45.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto raktapittapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.3"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.3x">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.45.3x</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vyāyāmabhārādhyayanavyavoyātapasevanaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tīkṣṇoṣṇakṣāralavaṇaiamlaiḥ kaṭvābhir eva ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.4"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.4x">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.45.4x</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         abhikṣṇaṃ sevato tūṣṇo rasaḥ pittaṃ pradūṣayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         pittaṃ vidagdhaṃ svaguṇaividahaty āśu śoṇitaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.5">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.45.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tataḥ pravartate raktamūrdhvaṃ cādho dvidhāpi vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         āmāśayād vrajed ūrdhvam adhaḥ pakvāśayād vrajet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.6ab">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.45.6ab</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vidagdhayoś cāpy ubhayor dvidhābhāgaṃ pravartate |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.7ab">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.45.7ab</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ūrdhvaṃ sādhyamadhoyāpyamasādhyaṃ yugapad gataṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.6cd">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.45.6cd</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yakṛn plīhāsyām ichanti kecid raktagatiṃ jānāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.7cd">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.45.7cd</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sadanaṃ śītakāmitvaṃ kaṇṭhadhūmāyanam vamī |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.8">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.45.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         lohagandhiś ca niśvāso bhavaty asmiṃ bhaviṣyati |
                        <caesura/>
                         vāhyāsṛglakṣaṇais tasya saṃkhyā doṣocchritair viduḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.9">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.45.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         daurvalyaśvāsakāsajvaravathumadā pāṇḍutādāhamūrcchā
                        <caesura/>
                         bhukte cānne vidāhas tv adhṛtir api sadā hṛdya tulyā ca pīḍā |
                        <caesura/>
                         tṛṣṇākaṇṭhasya bhedaḥ śirasi ca pavanaṃ pūtiniḥ ṣṭhīvanañ ca
                        <caesura/>
                         dveṣo bhakte vipāko viratir api bhaved raktapittopasargāt ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.10">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.45.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         māṃsaprakṣālanābhaṃ kvathitam api yakṛtkardamāñbhonibham vā
                        <caesura/>
                         medaḥ pūyāstikalpaṃ yakṛd iva yadi vā pakvajambūphalābham |
                        <caesura/>
                         yat kṛṣṇaṃ yac ca nīlaṃ bhṛśam atikuṇapaṃ yatra coktā vikārāḥ
                        <caesura/>
                         tad varjyaṃ raktapittaṃ surapatidhanuṣā yac ca tulyaṃ vibhāti
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.11">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.45.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nodṛktam ādau saṃgrāhyaṃ valino bhiṣaja sadā |
                        <caesura/>
                         hṛt pāṇḍugrahaṇīrogaplīhagulmajvarāvahaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.12">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.45.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         adhaḥ pravṛttaṃ vamanair ūrdhvagan tu virecanaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         jayed anyataraṃ cāpi kṣīṇasya śamanair asṛk |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.13"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.14"/>

                        <caesura/>
                         yaṣṭhīmadhukasiddhañ ca sakṣaudraṃ vamanaṃ hitaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.16">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.45.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         payāṃsi śītāni rasāś ca jāṅgalāḥ satīnamūdgāyavaśāliṣaṣṭikā |
                        <caesura/>
                         jīvanti śailūsuniṣaṇṇayūthikāṃs tathātimuktāṃ kura<damage
                            extent="4" unit="char"/>rajāḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.17">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.45.17</label>

                        dhātrīphaladāḍimānvitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         rasāś ca pārāvatahaṃsakurmajapeyā peyās tathā cāpi ghṛtāntarā
                        hitāḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.18">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.45.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         santānikāś cotpalapūrvakeṣu ghṛteṣu siddhāḥ payasaḥ sitāhvā |
                        <caesura/>
                         himāḥ pradehā madhurā gaṇāś ca ghṛtāni pathyāni ca raktapitte
                        |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.19">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.45.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         madhūkaśobhāñjanakodirajaiḥ priyaṃgukānāṃ kusumaiś ca cūrṇanitaḥ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhiṣag vidadhyāc caturaḥ samākṣikāṃ hitāya lehānasṛjāḥ praśāntaye
                        |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.20">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.45.20</label>
                        <caesura/>

                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         pathyāñ ca kharjūraphalaṃ samākṣikaṃ phalāni
                        cānyānyapitaṇguṇānyatha ||</l>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.23">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.45.23</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pivec chitakaṣāyaṃ vā jamvāmrārjunasambhavaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         āmodumvaraniryāsaṃ pibet sakṣaudraśarkaraṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.24">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.45.24</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         trapuśīmūlakalkam vā sakṣaudraṃ taṇḍutālāmvunā |
                        <caesura/>
                         pibed akṣasamaṃ kalkaṃ madhukalpaivam eva vā |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.25">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.45.25</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         candanaṃ padmaṃ kaṃlodhram evaṃ mevaṃ samaṃ pibet |
                        <caesura/>
                         karañjavījam evam vā sitākṣaudrayutaṃ pibet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.26">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.45.26</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         majjānamidgudasyaivam peyo madhukasaṃyutāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sukhoṣṇalavaṇaṃ vījaṃ karañjadadhimastunā |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.27">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.45.27</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pibed vāpi tryahaṃ martyo raktapittābhipīḍitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         raktapittaharāḥ śastāḥ ṣaḍete yogam uttamāḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.28">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.45.28</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pathyā caivāvapīḍeṣu grāṇataḥ pramṛte sṛji |
                        <caesura/>
                         atinissrutarakto vā kṣaudrayuktaṃ pibed asṛk |
                        <caesura/>
                         yakṛd vā bhakṣayed ājāmāṃsaṃ pittasamāyutaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.29">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.45.29</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         palāśavṛntasvarase vipakvaṃ
                        <caesura/>
                         sarpi pibet kṣaudrayutaṃ hitāśī |
                        <caesura/>
                         saśarkaraṃ kṣīraghṛtaṃ pibed vā
                        <caesura/>
                         vanaspatīṃ svarasaiḥ kṛtam vā |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.30">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.45.30</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         drākṣāmuśīrāṇy atha padmakaṃ sitā
                        <caesura/>
                         pṛthak palāṃśyudake samāvayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         sthitāṃ niśān tad rudhirāmayañ jayet
                        <caesura/>
                         pītaṃ payo vāmvusamaṃ hitāśinā |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.31">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.45.31</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         samākṣikaṃ vājiśakṛdrasaṃ vā
                        <caesura/>
                         vāsākaṣāyaṃ sahitaṃ pibed vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         lihyāt tathā vāstukavījacūrṇaṃ
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣaudraplutaṃ taṇḍulasāhvayam vā |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.32">

                        <caesura/>
                         liheta kālāñjanacūrṇām eva
                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
                         drāṣāsitātiktakarohiṇīñ ca
                        <caesura/>
                         himāmvunā vā madhukañ jayeyaṃ |</l>

                <div n="46" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 46: draft edition based on MS K]</head>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.46.1">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.46.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto mūrcchā pratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.46.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.46.3">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.46.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīṇasya bahudoṣasya viruddhāhārasevinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vegāghātād abhīghātād dhīnasatvasya vā punaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.46.4">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.46.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         karaṇāyataneṣūgrābāhyeṣv abhyantareṣu ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         niviśante yadā doṣās tadā mūrcchati mānavaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.46.5"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.46.6">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.46.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃjñāvahāsu nāḍīṣu pithitāsvanilādiṣu |
                        <caesura/>
                         tamobhyupaiti sahasā sukhadaḥkhavyapohakṛt |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.46.7">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.46.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sukhaduḥkhavyapohāc ca naraḥ naraḥ patati kāṣṭhavat |
                        <caesura/>
                         moho mūrcchati tām āhuḥ ṣaḍvidhā sā ca kīrtyate |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.46.8">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.46.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vātādibhiḥ śoṇitena madyena ca viśeṇa ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         ṣaṭsvetāsu ca paittīn tu prabhutvenāvatiṣṭhate |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.46.8.1">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.46.8.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         hṛtpīḍā jṛmbhaṇaṃ glāniḥ saṃjñādaurbalyam eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvāsāṃ pūrvarūpāṇi yathāsvañ ca vibhāvayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.46.9">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.46.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         apasmāraṇaliṅgāni tāsāmuktāni tatvataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pṛthivyāpastamorūpaṃ raktaṃ gandhaś ca tatra yaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.46.10">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.46.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmād raktasya gandhena mūrcchanti bhuvi mānavāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dravyasvabhāvam ity eke dṛṣṭvā yad api muhyati |</l>

                        <caesura/>
                         pibet mūtravikāraghnaṃ saṃsṛṣṭan tailamātrayeti || ❈ ||</l>

                        <caesura/>
                         tathāparaḥ śarkarayā sukaṣṭo mūtropaghātaḥ paṭhito ṣṭamas tu<del
                            rend="crossed out">ḥ</del> | </l>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.5">

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.60.1">

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.60.2">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.60.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ śṛṇu vatsa suśruta || <anchor
                            n="SS.6.60.2-n1"/>
                    </l>

                    <ab corresp="#SS.6.60.2" type="apparatus">
                        <list type="Notes">
                            <item corresp="#SS.6.60.2-n1"> One of the only two places in
                                the Nepalese version where this
                                    <foreign>yathovāca</foreign> phrase appears. The other
                                is Suśrutasaṃhitā 5.1.2. At that location, a scribe of
                                witness H added the marginal phrase <foreign>atha khalu
                                    vatsasuśrutaḥ</foreign>.</item>
                        </list>
                    </ab>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.60.3">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.60.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         niśācarebhyo rakṣyas tu nityam eva kṣatāturaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         iti yat prāgabhihitaṃ vistaran tasya vakṣyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.60.4">

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
                         kriyāś cāmānuṣī yasmiṃ sagrahaḥ parikīrttita<del>ā</del>ḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.60.5">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.60.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         aśucibhinnamayādakṣata taṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         hiṃsyur hiṃsāvihārārthaṃ satkārārtham athāpi vā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.60.6">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.60.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         asaṃkhyeyāṃ grahāṇyas ttu grahādhipatayas tu ye ||
                        <caesura/>
                         vyañjānte vividhākārā bhidyante te tathāṣṭadhā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.60.7">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.60.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         devās ca devārigaṇyas tathaiva gandharvayakṣāḥ pitaro bhujaṅgāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         rakṣāṃsi yā cāpi piśācahātireṣoṣṭako devagaṇyai grahaukhyaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.60.8">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.60.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃtuṣṭaḥ sucira vina ṣṭagandhamālyau nistandrīr
                        avitathasaṃskṛtābhilāpī |
                        <caesura/>
                         tejasvī sthitanayano varapradātā brahmaṇyau bhavati ca
                        rudradevajuṣṭaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.60.9">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.60.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃsvedīṃ dvijagurudevadoṣavaktā jihmākṣo vigatabhayo

                        <caesura/>
                         saṃtuṣṭo bhavati na cānnapānahātairdraṣṭātmā bhavati ca
                        devaśatrujuṣṭaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.60.10">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.60.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         hṛṣṭātmā pulinavanāntaropasevī svācāraḥ parigatagandhamālyapaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nṛttādyaiḥ prahasati cāru cālpaśabdaṃ gandharvagrahaparipīḍito
                        manuṣyaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.60.11">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.60.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tāmrākṣaḥ priyatanuraktavastradhārī gambhīro drutagatiralpavāk
                        sahiṣṇuḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         tejasvī vadati ca kim dadāmi kasmai yo yakṣagrahaparipīḍito
                        manuṣyaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.60.12">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.60.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pretānāṃ nipatati saṃstareṣu piṇḍāṃ śāntātmā jalam api

                        <caesura/>
                         māṃsepsustilakṛtapāyasābhikāmastadbhakṣo bhavati
                        pitṛgrahābhijuṣṭaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.60.13">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.60.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yastūrvyā prasarati sarpavat kadācit sṛkvaṇyau vilihati jihvayā
                        tathaiva ||
                        <caesura/>

                <div n="65" type="adhyāya">

                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 65: draft edition based on MS K]</head>

                    <head>[Adhyāya 65]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.1">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.65.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athātas tantrayuktyuddeśaṃ nāmādhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.3">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.65.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra dvātriṃśat tantrayuktayo bhavanti |
                        <caesura/>
                         tad yathā | adhikaraṇam | yogaḥ | padārthaḥ | hetvarthaḥ |
                        uddeśaḥ | nirdeśaḥ | upadeśaḥ | apadeśaḥ | pradeśaḥ | atideśaḥ |
                        apavargaḥ | vākyaśeṣaḥ | arthāpattiḥ | viparyayaḥ | prasaṅgaḥ |
                        ekāntaḥ | anekāntaḥ | pūrvapakṣaḥ | nirṇṇayaḥ | anumatam |
                        vidhānam | anāgatāpekṣaṇam | atikrāntāpekṣaṇaṃ | saṃśayaḥ |
                        vyākhyānam | svasaṃjñā | nirvacanam | nidarśanam | niyogaḥ |
                        vikalpaḥ | samuccayaḥ | ūhyam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.4">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.65.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atrāha | āsāṃ yuktīnāṃ kiṃ prayojanam | ucyate | vākyayojanam
                        arthayojanañ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.5">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.65.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ślokau cātra bhavataḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         asadvādiprayuktānāṃ<anchor n="SS.6.65.5-n1"/> śabdānāṃ
                        pratiṣedhanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         svavākyasiddhir api ca kriyate tantrayuktibhiḥ || </l>

                    <ab corresp="#SS.6.65.5" type="apparatus">
                        <list type="Note">
                            <item corresp="#SS.6.65.5-n1">We have adopted the vulgate
                                reading here, although it is highly unlikely to be
                                original. In MS H, this pāda appears to read <foreign
                                    xml:lang="sa">asadaprayuktānāñ ca</foreign>. This is
                                unmetrical, the compound is unusual, and there is an
                                unexplained <foreign xml:lang="sa">ca</foreign>. There
                                have been interventions in MS K by a second hand, and also
                                there is a hole in the manuscript just at this point. The
                                ante correctionem reading of K is unclear but appears to
                                be closer to the reading of H than to the vulgate reading.
                                These factors make it hard to reconstruct what a plausible
                                and correct older reading might have been. For the impact
                                on the meaning of this text, see notes to the
                                translation.</item>
                        </list>
                    </ab>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.6">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.65.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vyatyāsoktās tu ye hy arthā līnā ye cāpy anirmalāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         leśoktā ye ca kecit syus teṣāñ cāpi prasādhanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.7"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.8">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.65.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra yam artham adhikṛtyocyate tad adhikaraṇam | yathā rasaṃ
                        doṣaṃ vā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.9">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.65.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yena vākyaṃ yujyate sa yogaḥ | yathā vyatyāsenoktānāṃ
                        sannikṛṣṭaviprakṛṣṭānāṃ padārthānām ekīkaraṇam ||<anchor
                            n="#SS.6.65.9-n1"/>
                        <caesura/>
                         tailaṃ pibec cāmṛtavalli<pc> </pc><app>
                            <lem>nimba</lem>
                            <rdg wit="#JKT">vilva</rdg>
                        </app><pc> </pc><app>
                            <lem>haṃsāhvayā</lem>
                            <rdg wit="#JKT">hiṃsrābhayā</rdg>
                        </app><pc> </pc>vṛkṣakapippalībhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         siddhaṃ balābhyāñ ca sadevadāru hitāya nityaṃ galagaṇḍaroge
                            ||<anchor n="SS.6.65.9-n2"/>
                        <caesura/>
                         siddhaṃ pibed iti prathamaṃ vaktavye <app>
                            <lem>dvitīye pāde</lem>
                            <rdg wit="#JKT">tṛtīyapāde</rdg>
                        </app>
                        <app>
                            <lem>siddhaṃ</lem>
                            <rdg wit="#JKT">siddham iti</rdg>
                        </app> prayuktam |
                        <caesura/>
                         evan dūrasthānām api padārthānām ekīkaraṇaṃ yogaḥ || </l>

                    <ab corresp="#SS.6.65.9" type="apparatus">
                        <list type="Note">
                            <item corresp="#SS.6.65.9-n1">The sentence, <foreign>yathā...
                                    ekīkaraṇam </foreign>, does not appear in the vulgate
                                but an almost identical reading appears in Ḍalhana's
                                commentary on this section.</item>
                        </list>
                        <list type="Testimonia">

                            <item corresp="#SS.6.65.9-n2">
                                <ref
                                    target="https://saktumiva.org/wiki/wujastyk/susrutasamhita/04-su.ci-1-20/provisional-edition_cikitsasthana_01-20?upama_scroll=SS.4.18.47"
                                        ><foreign>Suśrutasaṃhitā 4.18.47</foreign></ref>.
                                For this section in the <foreign>Cikitsāsthāna</foreign>
                                there is only one witness viz., H, in the Nepalese
                                version. It has a minor variant reading in the second
                                line. Instead of <foreign>siddhaṃ balābhyāṃ ca
                                    sadevadāru</foreign>, it reads <foreign>siddhaṃ
                                    balābhyāṃ sahadevadāru</foreign>. The variant reading
                                in the vulgate as <foreign>°hiṃsrābhayā°</foreign> instead
                                of <foreign>haṃsāhvayā</foreign> is not found in the
                                actual occurrence of the verse in the
                                    <foreign>Cikitsāsthāna</foreign>, where it is
                                identical with its reading of the
                                    <foreign>tantrayukti</foreign> section in the Nepalese
                                version. The following quote from Vṛnda's
                                    <title>Siddhayoga</title> also supports the reading of
                                the Nepalese recension and the reading in the
                                    <foreign>Citkitsāsthāna</foreign> of the vulgate.
                                    <emph>Siddhayoga</emph>
                                <ref
                                    target="https://archive.org/details/VrndaMadhava1894/page/n171/mode/1up?view=theater"
                                    >41.10</ref>: <foreign>tailaṃ pibec
                                    cāmṛtavallinimbahaṃsāhvayāvṛkṣakapippalībhiḥ | siddhaṃ
                                    balābhyāṃ ca sadevadāru hitāya nityaṃ galagaṇḍaroge
                                    ||</foreign>
                            </item>
                        </list>
                    </ab>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.10">
                        <label>1938 ed. 6.65.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yo 'rtho 'bhihitaḥ sūtre pade<anchor n="SS.6.65.10-n1"/> vā sa
                        padārthaḥ | <app>
                            <lem>padasya padayoḥ padānāṃ vā yo 'rthaḥ sa padārthaḥ |</lem>
                            <rdg wit="#JKT"/>
                        </app> aparimitāś ca padārthāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yatra tu sneha<pc> </pc><app>
                            <lem>svedābhyañjaneṣu</lem>
                            <rdg wit="#JKT">svedāñjaneṣu nirddiṣṭeṣu</rdg>
                        </app> dvayos trayāṇāṃ vārthānām upapattir dṛśyate tatra yo 'rthaḥ
                            pūrvāparayoga<pc> </pc>siddho bhavati <app>
                            <lem>|</lem>
                            <rdg wit="#JKT">sa grahītavyaḥ |</rdg>
                        </app> yathā vedotpattim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma ity ukte sandihyate
                        buddhiḥ katamasya vedasyotpattiṃ <app>
                            <lem>vakṣyati</lem>
                            <rdg wit="#JKT">vivakṣur iti</rdg>
                        </app> | <app>
                            <lem>sāmavedādayaś ca</lem>
                            <rdg wit="#JKT">ṛgvedādayas tu</rdg>
                        </app> vedāḥ | <app>
                            <lem>pūrvāparam upalakṣya</lem>
                            <rdg wit="#JKT">pūrvāpara<pc> </pc>yogam upalabhya</rdg>
                        </app>
                        <app>
                            <lem>vinda vida</lem>
                            <rdg wit="#JKT">vid vicāraṇe vid vindati</rdg>
                        </app> ity etayoś ca dhātvor <app>
                            <lem>ekārthaḥ</lem>
                            <rdg wit="#JKT">anekārthayoḥ prayogaḥ</rdg>
                        </app> | paścāt <app>
                            <lem>padam</lem>
                            <rdg wit="#JKT">pratipattir</rdg>
                        </app> bhavati āyurvedotpattim ayaṃ vivakṣur iti <app>
                            <lem>eṣa</lem>
                            <rdg wit="#JKT">evaṃ</rdg>
                        </app> padārthaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.1"> athāto doṣabhedavikalpam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.3">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.4">

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l met="upajāti" xml:id="SS.6.66.17"> sahottaran tv etad adhītya
                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l met="Sragdharā" xml:id="SS.6.66.colophon2">
                        <label>6.66.colophon2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rājye śrīmānadeve pṛthusitayaśasi prodyadinduprakāśe
                        <caesura/>
                         kāle puṇyārjjanasya sakalajanamanohlādiramye vasante
                        <caesura/>
                         varṣe caikottare 'smiṃs tritayaśatagate mādhave māsi śukle
                        <caesura/>
                         saptamyāṃ puṣya ṛkṣe daśaśatakiraṇe vāsare siddhayoge |</l>

                    <l met="Sragdharā" xml:id="SS.6.66.colophon3">
                        <label>6.66.colophon3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         utpattyādyambuvelākulavividharujagrāhajuṣṭātiraudre
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃsāre sāgare 'smiñ jagad idam akhilaṃ glāninam sampravīkṣya
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmāc chrīharṣacandro niratiśayaghṛṇābhāvito moktukāmaḥ
                        <caesura/>
                         prītyā caigaṃ <sic>prākhilat</sic> suśrutākhyam |<anchor
                            n="SS.6.66.colophon3-n1"/>
                    </l>

                    <ab corresp="#SS.6.66.colophon3" type="apparatus">
                        <list type="Notes">
                            <item corresp="#SS.6.66.colophon3-n1">It is hard to understand how a word ending in
                                    <foreign>-gaṃ</foreign>, or any accusative, could
                                precede <foreign>prākhilat</foreign> or even <foreign>pra
                                    akhilan</foreign>. Some readers have emended <foreign
                                    xml:lang="sa">prākhilat</foreign> to <foreign
                                    xml:lang="sa">prālikhat</foreign>, a rare verb, but
                                one that at least governs the accusative. We do not see
                                metathesis elsewhere in the work of K's scribe, which is
                                generally very accurate, so we consider the emendation
                                unlikely. With so many words missing from this passage, we
                                consider that emendation is not useful.</item>

                            <item>We read <foreign>-harṣacandro</foreign> which could be
                                the name of the scribe. But the following
                                    <foreign>nnirati-</foreign> is hard to construe. If we
                                read the ablative <foreign>-harṣacandrān</foreign>, it
                                solve the problem of <foreign>-nn-</foreign> but is also
                                hard to construe.</item>
                        </list>
                    </ab>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.colophon4">
                        <label>6.66.colophon4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śrīgaṇadevadevakuladūnī gvalakanivāsino vaidyavasuvarmaṇaḥ
                        pustakam idaṃ paṭhitvārtham avagamya sarvasattvānām upadeśaṃ
                        vidhātuṃ pratipāditam | atas tad ādhikrayābhyāṃ tad gotrajena
                        kenacin na kañcid dātavyam | yadā nopakriyate tadāsmān eva
                        pratyarpaṇīyam iti || </l>


                </div>

            </div>
        </body>
    </text>
